## 英文自然拼读课程（200词 / 6阶段）

基于 Jolly Phonics 42音素系统 + Dolch Sight Words + K-1 名词。
共 **6** 个阶段，**200** 个词汇。

### Stage 1: Core Phonemes（核心音素）

| 词 | 音素 | 类型 | 例句 |
|---|------|------|------|
| s | /s/ | 字母音 | S is for sun. |
| a | /æ/ | 字母音 | A is for apple. |
| t | /t/ | 字母音 | T is for ten. |
| p | /p/ | 字母音 | P is for pot. |
| i | /ɪ/ | 字母音 | I is for ink. |
| n | /n/ | 字母音 | N is for net. |
| ck | /k/ | 字母音 | Ck is for duck. |
| e | /e/ | 字母音 | E is for egg. |
| h | /h/ | 字母音 | H is for hat. |
| r | /r/ | 字母音 | R is for rat. |
| m | /m/ | 字母音 | M is for map. |
| d | /d/ | 字母音 | D is for dog. |
| g | /g/ | 字母音 | G is for goat. |
| o | /ɒ/ | 字母音 | O is for ox. |
| u | /ʌ/ | 字母音 | U is for up. |
| l | /l/ | 字母音 | L is for leg. |
| f | /f/ | 字母音 | F is for fish. |
| b | /b/ | 字母音 | B is for banana. |

| and | /æ/ /n/ /d/ | 高频词 | A cat and a dog. |
| can | /k/ /æ/ /n/ | 高频词 | I can run fast. |
| go | /g/ /əʊ/ | 高频词 | Go, go, go! |

| to | /t/ /uː/ | 高频词 | I go to bed. |
| not | /n/ /ɒ/ /t/ | 高频词 | The ant is not big. |
| big | /b/ /ɪ/ /g/ | 高频词 | The dog is big. |
| me | /m/ /iː/ | 高频词 | Hug me! |

### Stage 4: Digraphs & Blends（双辅音与合音）

| 词 | 音素 | 类型 | 例句 |
|---|------|------|------|
| ship | /ʃ/ /ɪ/ /p/ | 双辅音 | Look at the ship. |
| shop | /ʃ/ /ɒ/ /p/ | 双辅音 | This is a shop. |
| fish | /f/ /ɪ/ /ʃ/ | 双辅音 | The fish is here. |
| chip | /tʃ/ /ɪ/ /p/ | 双辅音 | I like the chip. |
| chin | /tʃ/ /ɪ/ /n/ | 双辅音 | This is my chin. |

## 其他语言词汇课程

共 **13** 种语言。每种语言 **172** 个词汇，分为 **5** 个学习阶段。

#### Stage 5: Tense & Aspirated Consonants — 30 words

| 词 | 音素 | 类型 | 中文释义 | 例句 |
|---|------|------|---------|------|
